A touch target of 48x48dp results in a physical size of about 9mm, regardless of screen size, and the recommended target size for touchscreen objects is 7-10mm.\n\n## Spacing Between Touch Targets\n\nTouch targets should be separated by 8dp of space or more to ensure balanced information density and usability. In most cases, there should be 8dp or more space between them.\n\n## Implementation\n\nThese guidelines are described in the Material Design Accessibility guidelines. For implementation, developers can use `android:minWidth` and `android:minHeight` attributes to ensure minimum touch target dimensions, or use `TouchDelegate` to expand the touchable region while retaining the original visual size of a view.\n\n## Special Context: Automotive\n\nIt's worth noting that for automotive interfaces, the requirements are different. As per Google Design for Driving guidelines, the minimum touch target size is 76dp * 76dp due to the safety-critical nature of in-car interactions."}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ba2f6b21-1f26-4fe6-aa5a-a0339243fb2d","uuid":"17872952-ac87-4934-aca1-0a63015d2bf8"}

A touch target of 48x48dp results in a physical size of about 9mm, regardless of screen size.\n\nApple's Human Interface Guidelines recommend a minimum target size of 44 pixels wide by 44 pixels tall, though some designers consider this a bare minimum.\n\n## Button Spacing\n\nTouch targets should be separated by 8dp/16px of space or more to ensure balanced information density and usability. This spacing helps prevent accidental taps on adjacent buttons.\n\nTo avoid accidental taps, targets must first be big enough, and then also spaced well enough. Small spacing can cause issues even when buttons meet minimum size requirements.\n\n## Context-Dependent Sizing\n\nResearch suggests aiming for 11mm (or 31pt / 42px) at the top of the screen, and 12mm (or 34pt / 46px) at the bottom of the screen to minimize rage taps. In the center of the screen, you could potentially go as low as 7mm (or 20pt / 27px).\n\n## Key Takeaways\n\n- **Minimum size**: 48x48dp for Material Design, 44x44px for iOS\n- **Spacing**: At least 8dp between touch targets\n- **Physical size**: Aim for 7-10mm physically on screen\n- Location matters: Larger targets needed at screen edges than in the center"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ba2f6b21-1f26-4fe6-aa5a-a0339243fb2d","uuid":"0db05d09-82ac-4107-b4af-1a3db8e9f9c0"}
